  <script>
   $.fn.counting = function (opts) {
            let defaults = {
                from: 0,
                to: null,
                easing: 'swing',
                fade: true,
                complete: null
            };
            let options = $.extend(defaults, opts);

            function format(num) {
                num = num.toFixed();
                return num
            }

            return this.each(function () {
                let obj = $(this);
                let from = options.from;
                if (obj.attr('data-from')) {
                    from = parseFloat(obj.attr('data-from'));
                }
                let to = options.to;
                if (obj.attr('data-to')) {
                    to = parseFloat(obj.attr('data-to'));
                }
                let duration = options.duration;

                obj.css('counter', from);
                if (options.fade) obj.css('opacity', 0.7);
                obj.animate(
                        {
                            counter: to,
                            opacity: 1
                        },
                        {
                            easing: options.easing,
                            duration: duration,

                            step: function (progress) {
                                obj.html(format(progress * to));
                            },
                            complete: function () {
                                obj.css('counter', null);
                                obj.html(format(to));
                                if (options.complete) {
                                    options.complete(obj)
                                }
                            }
                        }
                )
            })
        }
  </script>

     <p>
      DatingStudio focuses on the niche dating and assists singles who have a clear vision of a specific category of partners he or she is attracted by. On our portal, you will not find reviews on
        all dating sites available online but you will get an access to the analysis of niche matchmaking websites. If you are a single parent, if you are interested in meeting an experienced woman,
        if you want to date a person of a different race or if you have any other demands we will help you.
     </p>
     <p>
      DatingStudio covers all the popular niche dating categories: for each category, we have selected several websites that offer top-rated services and have a remarkable reputation among
        customers. We believe that if you are looking for love we are able to provide you with exactly what you need. Just look through the list and choose the appealing category!
     </p>

           <h3>
            Where to Find the Best Dating Service?
           </h3>
           <p>
            As the number of
            <strong>
             international dating sites
            </strong>
            is pretty impressive it might seem that there is nothing easier than to choose one and start chatting with other users.
                                But such an attitude towards the selection of an
            <strong>
             online dating service
            </strong>
            is risky and might cost you a fortune. The dating market attracts lots of fraudsters that take
                                advantage of naÃ¯ve newbies. Apparently, you have no desire to be added to the list of victims. To avoid such destiny you have to be critical when looking through
            <strong>
             dating sites
            </strong>
            .
                                You should pay attention only to those portals that are among the top-rated providers and that can brag of a flawless reputation. Hence, to find a perfect dating venue you should check out the
                                rankings reflecting an attitude of clients and experts towards the selected websites. Only due to several top-lists you would be able to detect a site or a few sites that suit your needs and
                                that prove to be decent.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="slider_inactive slider_unit" id="slide_2">
           <h3>
            How to Start Your Pursuit of Love?
           </h3>
           <p>
            If you know which niche category you are interested in you should come up with your personal list of
            <strong>
             top 5 dating sites
            </strong>
            . To complete the one you are expected to give a
                                try to a few
            <strong>
             matchmaking services
            </strong>
            which you have already selected: you need to make sure that the site has a convenient interface, that the interaction tools are of a high
                                quality, that the number of users satisfies you and that the price you pay for the services you get is fair. Considering all the nuances meet your expectations, you are ready to begin the
                                adventure and to
            <strong>
             find love online
            </strong>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            First of all, you need an informative and appealing profile: do not miss a chance to add your photo and to share a few words about a perfect partner you wish to meet. Also, you must be ready
                                to
                                make a first step towards the user you find attractive â€“ do not hesitate and try to start a conversation. If you wait for someone to contact you, you might lose lots of opportunities. And do
                                not neglect incoming messages: you never know if it is a random person sending random messages to random people or if it is your true love.
           </p>
           <p>
            Hence, the secret is simple â€“ do not be scared or shy and talk to people as much as you can.
           </p>

            Why Should You Give It a Try?
           </h3>

            An experienced
            <strong>
             matchmaker
            </strong>

                                people and leave them dreaming about happiness instead of making them happy. If you want to break this vicious circle we recommend you to stop dreaming and to start acting!
           </p>

            Indeed, to
            <strong>

            </strong>

                                would make your life easier. Do not miss your chance for happiness!

       <h2>
        Online dating
       </h2>
       <div class="toggle_icon">
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq_toggle">
       <p>
        Online dating becomes more and more widespread every day, there is nothing easier than finding yourself a partner online. People in the 21st century care about their time and resource, thatâ€™s why they prefer to get involved into dating that is more likely to end up successfully.
       </p>
       <p>
        Here on DatingStudio we provide you with the best dating venues to use. But how can you be sure that it is effective?
       </p>
       <p>
        Our experts have carefully selected the top sites which surely lead to the happy ending. Moreover, as long as you know exactly how online dating works, youâ€™ll be able to figure out the best website for you.
       </p>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="faq_block">
      <div class="faq_click">
       <h3>
        Why is online dating effective?
       </h3>
       <div class="toggle_icon">
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="faq_toggle">
       <p>
        Letâ€™s dive deeper into the working algorithms of online dating. There are a few reasons that makes it efficient and beneficial for the users. Moreover, it is suitable for everyone.        </p>
       <h4>
        Reason 1. It is simple

       <p>
        There are no troubles with the registration on a dating site, and the further communication is also a piece of cake. Yet, it doesnâ€™t cause any difficulties. And it is pretty natural for men and women to flirt, talk and exchange opinions on different topics.

       <h4>
        Reason 2. It is specialized.
       </h4>
       <p>
        When you come to date online, you usually know exactly who you want. Moreover, you come for a certain type of relationship. Dating Studio is ready to help you with dating in various categories. You can find them all here! Whatever you want, you can find it here. Both serious relationships and one-night stands are easy to get if you use Dating Studio. The team f experts carefully selects the best sites in each niche and makes sure that every customer is about to get what they came for.
       </p>
       <h4>
        Reason 3. It has an aim.

        Say goodbye to long pointless dates. Online dating is almost a 100% guarantee that you wonâ€™t waste any time and money. Here, anybody can find a site and a partner to their taste.         </li>
        <li>
         Find a website that meets your demands. Reading some reviews beforehand is a great idea.
        </li>

        </li>
        <li>
         Look through the profiles of your potential dates and text a couple of them.
        </li>
        <li>
         Develop the communication and choose 2 or 3 people you like most.
        </li>

        </li>

        function refreshOnline() {
            $('.counter').each(function () {
                let obj = $(this);
                let refreshing = setInterval(function () {
                    let toOld = obj.attr('data-to');
                    let oldFrom = obj.attr('data-from');
                    let newFrom = obj.attr('data-from').replace(oldFrom, toOld);
                    let refreshto = 0;
                    let randomnumber = Math.floor(Math.random() * 50);
                    if (randomnumber % 2 == 0) {
                        refreshto = parseFloat(toOld) + Math.floor(Math.random() * 5);
                    }
                    else {
                        refreshto = parseFloat(toOld) - Math.floor(Math.random() * 5);
                    }

                    let toNew = obj.attr('data-to').replace(toOld, refreshto.toString());
                    obj.attr('data-from', newFrom);
                    obj.attr('data-to', toNew);
                    if (refreshto > 20000) clearInterval(refreshing);
                    obj.counting({
                        duration: 2000,
                        fade: false
                    });
                }, 20000);
            });

        }

        refreshOnline();
        var slide_1 = $('#slide_1');
        var slide_2 = $('#slide_2');
        var slide_3 = $('#slide_3');
        var left_arrow = $('#left_arrow');
        var right_arrow = $('#right_arrow');
        var slider_counter = 1;

        left_arrow.on('click', function () {
            if (slider_counter == 1) {
                slider_counter = 3;
                slide_3.addClass("slider_active");
                slide_3.removeClass("slider_inactive");
                slide_1.addClass("slider_inactive");
                slide_2.addClass("slider_inactive");
                return false;
            }
            // slider_counter = 3;

            if (slider_counter == 2) {
                slider_counter = 1;

                slide_1.addClass("slider_active");
                slide_1.removeClass("slider_inactive");

                slide_2.addClass("slider_inactive");
                slide_2.removeClass("slider_active");

                slide_3.addClass("slider_inactive");
                slide_3.removeClass("slider_active");
                return false;
            }

            if (slider_counter == 3) {
                slider_counter = 2;
                slide_2.addClass("slider_active");
                slide_2.removeClass("slider_inactive");
                slide_1.addClass("slider_inactive");
                slide_3.addClass("slider_inactive");
                return false;
            }
        });

        right_arrow.on('click', function () {
            if (slider_counter == 1) {

                slide_2.removeClass("slider_inactive");

                slide_3.addClass("slider_inactive");
                return false;

                slide_1.removeClass("slider_active");
